       y f xx yy ff)

(**
 3. Preservation of opcartesian 2-cells

Section LocalOpCartesianOpFibration.
  Context {C₁ C₂ : bicat_of_univ_cats}
          {F₁ F₂ : C₁ --> C₂}
          (α : F₁ ==> F₂)
          {D₁ : disp_bicat_of_opcleaving C₁}
          {D₂ : disp_bicat_of_opcleaving C₂}
          {FF₁ : D₁ -->[ F₁ ] D₂}
          {FF₂ : D₁ -->[ F₂ ] D₂}
          (αα : disp_2cells α FF₁ FF₂)
          (Hαα : ∏ (x : C₁ : univalent_category)
                   (xx : (pr1 D₁ : disp_univalent_category _) x),
                 is_opcartesian ((pr11 αα) x xx))
          (G : bicat_of_univ_cats
                 ⟦ total_univalent_category (pr1 D₁)
                   ,
                   total_univalent_category (pr1 D₂) ⟧)
          (tot_FF₁ := (total_functor (pr1 FF₁)
                       : bicat_of_univ_cats
                           ⟦ total_univalent_category (pr1 D₁)
                             ,
                             total_univalent_category (pr1 D₂) ⟧))
          (tot_FF₂ := (total_functor (pr1 FF₂)
                       : bicat_of_univ_cats
                           ⟦ total_univalent_category (pr1 D₁)
                             ,
                             total_univalent_category (pr1 D₂) ⟧))
          (tot_αα := total_nat_trans (pr1 αα) : tot_FF₁ ==> tot_FF₂)
          (γ : tot_FF₁ ==> G)
          (δp : tot_FF₂ · pr1_category _ ==> G · pr1_category _)
          (q : post_whisker γ (pr1_category (pr11 D₂))
               =
               nat_trans_comp
                 _ _ _
                 (post_whisker (total_nat_trans (pr1 αα)) (pr1_category _))
                 δp).

                                                 (pr1
                                                 y),
                                                 pr1
                                                 (G y)
                                                 ⟧,
                                                 pr1
                                                 FF₁
                                                 (pr1
                                                 y)
                                                 (pr2
                                                 y) -->[
                                                 z] 
                                                 pr2
                                                 (G y))
                                                 (nat_trans_eq_pointwise
                                                 q y)
                                                 (pr2
                                                 (pr1
                                                 γ y))))))%mor_disp =
((pr11 αα) (pr1 x) (pr2 x) ;; pr2
                                (pr1 δp x
                                 · pr1
                                     ((# (pr1 G))%cat
                                        f),,
                                 opcartesian_factorisation
                                   (Hαα (pr1 x)
                                      (pr2 x))
                                   (pr1 δp x)
                                   (transportf
                                      (λ z : C₂
                                             ⟦ F₁
                                                 (pr1
                                                 x),
                                             pr1 (G x)
                                             ⟧,
                                       pr1 FF₁ (pr1 x)
                                         (pr2 x) -->[
                                       z] pr2 (G x))
                                      (nat_trans_eq_pointwise
                                         q x)
                                      (pr2 (pr1 γ x))) ;; 
                                 pr2
                                   ((# (pr1 G))%cat f)))%mor_disp

      
C₁, C₂: bicat_of_univ_cats
F₁, F₂: bicat_of_univ_cats ⟦ C₁, C₂ ⟧
α: F₁ ==> F₂
D₁: disp_bicat_of_opcleaving C₁
D₂: disp_bicat_of_opcleaving C₂
FF₁: D₁ -->[ F₁] D₂
FF₂: D₁ -->[ F₂] D₂
αα: disp_2cells α FF₁ FF₂
Hαα: ∏ (x : C₁ : univalent_category)
(xx : (pr1 D₁ : disp_univalent_category C₁) x),
is_opcartesian ((pr11 αα) x xx)
G: bicat_of_univ_cats
⟦ total_univalent_category (pr1 D₁),
total_univalent_category (pr1 D₂) ⟧

⟦ total_univalent_category (pr1 D₁),
total_univalent_category (pr1 D₂) ⟧

⟦ total_univalent_category (pr1 D₁),
total_univalent_category (pr1 D₂) ⟧
tot_αα:= total_nat_trans (pr1 αα): tot_FF₁ ==> tot_FF₂
γ: tot_FF₁ ==> G
δp: tot_FF₂ · pr1_category (pr1 D₂) ==>
G · pr1_category (pr1 D₂)
q: post_whisker γ (pr1_category (pr11 D₂)) =
nat_trans_comp
  (functor_composite_data
     (total_functor (pr1 FF₁))
     (pr1_category (pr1 D₂)))
  (functor_composite_data
     (total_functor (pr1 FF₂))
     (pr1_category (pr1 D₂)))
  (G · pr1_category (pr1 D₂))
  (post_whisker (total_nat_trans (pr1 αα))
     (pr1_category (pr1 D₂))) δp
x, y: total_univalent_category (pr1 D₁)
f: total_univalent_category (pr1 D₁) ⟦ x, y ⟧
((pr11 αα) (pr1 x) (pr2 x) ;; transportf
                                (mor_disp
                                   (pr1 FF₂ (pr1 x)
                                      (pr2 x))
                                   (pr2 (pr1 G y)))
                                (nat_trans_ax δp x y f)
                                (♯ (pr1 FF₂) (pr2 f) ;; 
                                 opcartesian_factorisation

                                      (pr2 y))

                                         (pr2 y) -->[
                                       z] pr2 (G y))
                                      (nat_trans_eq_pointwise
                                         q y)
                                      (pr2 (pr1 γ y)))))%mor_disp =
((pr11 αα) (pr1 x) (pr2 x) ;; (opcartesian_factorisation
                                 (Hαα (pr1 x) (pr2 x))
                                 (pr1 δp x)

                                    (λ z : C₂

                                       (pr2 x) -->[

                               pr2 ((# (pr1 G))%cat f)))%mor_disp

tot_αα:= total_nat_trans (pr1 αα): tot_FF₁ ==> tot_FF₂
γ: tot_FF₁ ==> G
δp: tot_FF₂ · pr1_category (pr1 D₂) ==>
G · pr1_category (pr1 D₂)
q: post_whisker γ (pr1_category (pr11 D₂)) =
nat_trans_comp
  (functor_composite_data
     (total_functor (pr1 FF₁))
     (pr1_category (pr1 D₂)))
  (functor_composite_data
     (total_functor (pr1 FF₂))
     (pr1_category (pr1 D₂)))
  (G · pr1_category (pr1 D₂))
  (post_whisker (total_nat_trans (pr1 αα))
     (pr1_category (pr1 D₂))) δp
x, y: total_univalent_category (pr1 D₁)
f: total_univalent_category (pr1 D₁) ⟦ x, y ⟧
transportf
  (mor_disp (pr1 FF₁ (pr1 x) (pr2 x)) (pr2 (pr1 G y)))
  (! assoc (α (pr1 x)) (# F₂ (pr1 f)) (pr1 δp y) @
   maponpaths (compose (α (pr1 x)))
     (nat_trans_ax δp x y f))
  ((pr11 αα) (pr1 x) (pr2 x) ;; ♯ (pr1 FF₂) (pr2 f) ;; 
   opcartesian_factorisation (Hαα (pr1 y) (pr2 y))
     (pr1 δp y)
     (transportf
        (λ z : C₂ ⟦ F₁ (pr1 y), pr1 (G y) ⟧,
         pr1 FF₁ (pr1 y) (pr2 y) -->[ z] pr2 (G y))
        (nat_trans_eq_pointwise q y) (pr2 (pr1 γ y))))%mor_disp =
transportf
  (mor_disp (pr1 FF₁ (pr1 x) (pr2 x)) (pr2 (pr1 G y)))
  (! assoc (α (pr1 x)) (pr1 δp x) (pr1 (# (pr1 G) f)))
  (transportf
     (λ z : C₂ ⟦ F₁ (pr1 x), pr1 (G x) ⟧,
      pr1 FF₁ (pr1 x) (pr2 x) -->[ z] pr2 (G x))
     (nat_trans_eq_pointwise q x) (pr2 (pr1 γ x)) ;; 
   pr2 ((# (pr1 G))%cat f))%mor_disp

α: F₁ ==> F₂
D₁: disp_bicat_of_opcleaving C₁
D₂: disp_bicat_of_opcleaving C₂
FF₁: D₁ -->[ F₁] D₂
FF₂: D₁ -->[ F₂] D₂
αα: disp_2cells α FF₁ FF₂
Hαα: ∏ (x : C₁ : univalent_category)
(xx : (pr1 D₁ : disp_univalent_category C₁) x),
is_opcartesian ((pr11 αα) x xx)
G: bicat_of_univ_cats
⟦ total_univalent_category (pr1 D₁),
total_univalent_category (pr1 D₂) ⟧
tot_FF₁:= total_functor (pr1 FF₁): bicat_of_univ_cats
⟦ total_univalent_category (pr1 D₁),
total_univalent_category (pr1 D₂) ⟧
tot_FF₂:= total_functor (pr1 FF₂): bicat_of_univ_cats
⟦ total_univalent_category (pr1 D₁),
total_univalent_category (pr1 D₂) ⟧
tot_αα:= total_nat_trans (pr1 αα): tot_FF₁ ==> tot_FF₂
γ: tot_FF₁ ==> G
δp: tot_FF₂ · pr1_category (pr1 D₂) ==>
G · pr1_category (pr1 D₂)
q: post_whisker γ (pr1_category (pr11 D₂)) =
nat_trans_comp
  (functor_composite_data
     (total_functor (pr1 FF₁))
     (pr1_category (pr1 D₂)))
  (functor_composite_data
     (total_functor (pr1 FF₂))
     (pr1_category (pr1 D₂)))
  (G · pr1_category (pr1 D₂))
  (post_whisker (total_nat_trans (pr1 αα))
     (pr1_category (pr1 D₂))) δp
x, y: total_univalent_category (pr1 D₁)
f: total_univalent_category (pr1 D₁) ⟦ x, y ⟧
transportf
  (mor_disp (pr1 FF₁ (pr1 x) (pr2 x)) (pr2 (pr1 G y)))
  (! assoc (α (pr1 x)) (# F₂ (pr1 f)) (pr1 δp y) @
   maponpaths (compose (α (pr1 x)))
     (nat_trans_ax δp x y f))
  (transportf
     (mor_disp (pr1 FF₁ (pr1 x) (pr2 x))
        (pr1 FF₂ (pr1 y) (pr2 y)))
     (nat_trans_ax α (pr1 x) (pr1 y) (pr1 f))
     (♯ (pr1 FF₁) (pr2 f) ;; pr1 αα (pr1 y) (pr2 y)) ;; 
   opcartesian_factorisation (Hαα (pr1 y) (pr2 y))
     (pr1 δp y)
     (transportf
        (λ z : C₂ ⟦ F₁ (pr1 y), pr1 (G y) ⟧,
         pr1 FF₁ (pr1 y) (pr2 y) -->[ z] pr2 (G y))
        (nat_trans_eq_pointwise q y) (pr2 (pr1 γ y))))%mor_disp =
transportf
  (mor_disp (pr1 FF₁ (pr1 x) (pr2 x)) (pr2 (pr1 G y)))
  (cancel_postcomposition (pr1 (pr1 γ x))
     (α (pr1 x) · pr1 δp x) (pr1 (# (pr1 G) f))
     (nat_trans_eq_pointwise q x) @
   ! assoc (α (pr1 x)) (pr1 δp x) (pr1 (# (pr1 G) f)))
  (pr2 (pr1 γ x) ;; pr2 ((# (pr1 G))%cat f))%mor_disp

  (♯ (pr1 FF₁) (pr2 f) ;; pr2 (pr1 γ y))%mor_disp =
transportf
  (mor_disp (pr1 FF₁ (pr1 x) (pr2 x)) (pr2 (pr1 G y)))
  (cancel_postcomposition (pr1 (pr1 γ x))
     (α (pr1 x) · pr1 δp x) (pr1 (# (pr1 G) f))
     (nat_trans_eq_pointwise q x) @
   ! assoc (α (pr1 x)) (pr1 δp x) (pr1 (# (pr1 G) f)))
  (pr2 (pr1 γ x) ;; pr2 ((# (pr1 G))%cat f))%mor_disp

D₂: disp_bicat_of_opcleaving C₂

C₁, C₂: bicat_of_univ_cats
F₁, F₂: bicat_of_univ_cats ⟦ C₁, C₂ ⟧
α: F₁ ==> F₂
D₁: disp_bicat_of_opcleaving C₁
D₂: disp_bicat_of_opcleaving C₂
FF₁: D₁ -->[ F₁] D₂
FF₂: D₁ -->[ F₂] D₂
αα: disp_2cells α FF₁ FF₂
Hαα: ∏ (x : C₁ : univalent_category)
(xx : (pr1 D₁ : disp_univalent_category C₁) x),
is_opcartesian ((pr11 αα) x xx)
G: bicat_of_univ_cats
⟦ total_univalent_category (pr1 D₁),
total_univalent_category (pr1 D₂) ⟧
tot_FF₁:= total_functor (pr1 FF₁): bicat_of_univ_cats
⟦ total_univalent_category (pr1 D₁),
total_univalent_category (pr1 D₂) ⟧
tot_FF₂:= total_functor (pr1 FF₂): bicat_of_univ_cats
⟦ total_univalent_category (pr1 D₁),
total_univalent_category (pr1 D₂) ⟧
tot_αα:= total_nat_trans (pr1 αα): tot_FF₁ ==> tot_FF₂
γ: tot_FF₁ ==> G
δp: tot_FF₂ · pr1_category (pr1 D₂) ==>
G · pr1_category (pr1 D₂)
q: post_whisker γ (pr1_category (pr11 D₂)) =
nat_trans_comp
  (functor_composite_data
     (total_functor (pr1 FF₁))
     (pr1_category (pr1 D₂)))
  (functor_composite_data
     (total_functor (pr1 FF₂))
     (pr1_category (pr1 D₂)))
  (G · pr1_category (pr1 D₂))
  (post_whisker (total_nat_trans (pr1 αα))
     (pr1_category (pr1 D₂))) δp
x, y: total_univalent_category (pr1 D₁)
f: total_univalent_category (pr1 D₁) ⟦ x, y ⟧
! base_paths (# tot_FF₁ f · γ y) (γ x · # G f)
    (nat_trans_ax γ x y f) @
maponpaths (compose (# F₁ (pr1 f)))
  (nat_trans_eq_pointwise q y) @
assoc (# F₁ (pr1 f)) (α (pr1 y)) (pr1 δp y) @
cancel_postcomposition (# F₁ (pr1 f) · α (pr1 y))
  (α (pr1 x) · # F₂ (pr1 f)) (pr1 δp y)
  (nat_trans_ax α (pr1 x) (pr1 y) (pr1 f)) @
! assoc (α (pr1 x)) (# F₂ (pr1 f)) (pr1 δp y) @
maponpaths (compose (α (pr1 x)))
  (nat_trans_ax δp x y f) =
cancel_postcomposition (pr1 (pr1 γ x))
  (α (pr1 x) · pr1 δp x) (pr1 (# (pr1 G) f))
  (nat_trans_eq_pointwise q x) @
! assoc (α (pr1 x)) (pr1 δp x) (pr1 (# (pr1 G) f))

      apply homset_property.
  Qed.

  
C₁, C₂: bicat_of_univ_cats
F₁, F₂: bicat_of_univ_cats ⟦ C₁, C₂ ⟧
α: F₁ ==> F₂
D₁: disp_bicat_of_opcleaving C₁
D₂: disp_bicat_of_opcleaving C₂
FF₁: D₁ -->[ F₁] D₂
FF₂: D₁ -->[ F₂] D₂
αα: disp_2cells α FF₁ FF₂
Hαα: ∏ (x : C₁ : univalent_category)
(xx : (pr1 D₁ : disp_univalent_category C₁) x),
is_opcartesian ((pr11 αα) x xx)
G: bicat_of_univ_cats
⟦ total_univalent_category (pr1 D₁),
total_univalent_category (pr1 D₂) ⟧
tot_FF₁:= total_functor (pr1 FF₁): bicat_of_univ_cats
⟦ total_univalent_category (pr1 D₁),
total_univalent_category (pr1 D₂) ⟧
tot_FF₂:= total_functor (pr1 FF₂): bicat_of_univ_cats
⟦ total_univalent_category (pr1 D₁),
total_univalent_category (pr1 D₂) ⟧
tot_αα:= total_nat_trans (pr1 αα): tot_FF₁ ==> tot_FF₂
γ: tot_FF₁ ==> G
δp: tot_FF₂ · pr1_category (pr1 D₂) ==>
G · pr1_category (pr1 D₂)
q: post_whisker γ (pr1_category (pr11 D₂)) =
nat_trans_comp
  (functor_composite_data
     (total_functor (pr1 FF₁))
     (pr1_category (pr1 D₂)))

     (total_functor (pr1 FF₂))
     (pr1_category (pr1 D₂)))
  (G · pr1_category (pr1 D₂))

     (pr1_category (pr1 D₂))) δp
tot_FF₂ ==> G

αα: disp_2cells α FF₁ FF₂
Hαα: ∏ (x : C₁ : univalent_category)
(xx : (pr1 D₁ : disp_univalent_category C₁) x),
is_opcartesian ((pr11 αα) x xx)
G: bicat_of_univ_cats
⟦ total_univalent_category (pr1 D₁),
total_univalent_category (pr1 D₂) ⟧
tot_FF₁:= total_functor (pr1 FF₁): bicat_of_univ_cats
⟦ total_univalent_category (pr1 D₁),
total_univalent_category (pr1 D₂) ⟧
tot_FF₂:= total_functor (pr1 FF₂): bicat_of_univ_cats
⟦ total_univalent_category (pr1 D₁),
total_univalent_category (pr1 D₂) ⟧
tot_αα:= total_nat_trans (pr1 αα): tot_FF₁ ==> tot_FF₂
γ: tot_FF₁ ==> G
δp: tot_FF₂ · pr1_category (pr1 D₂) ==>
G · pr1_category (pr1 D₂)
q: post_whisker γ (pr1_category (pr11 D₂)) =
nat_trans_comp
  (functor_composite_data
     (total_functor (pr1 FF₁))
     (pr1_category (pr1 D₂)))
  (functor_composite_data
     (total_functor (pr1 FF₂))
     (pr1_category (pr1 D₂)))
  (G · pr1_category (pr1 D₂))
  (post_whisker (total_nat_trans (pr1 αα))
     (pr1_category (pr1 D₂))) δp
∏ x : total_univalent_category (pr1 D₁),
(tot_αα • local_opcartesian_opcleaving_lift) x = γ x

F₁, F₂: bicat_of_univ_cats ⟦ C₁, C₂ ⟧
α: F₁ ==> F₂
D₁: disp_bicat_of_opcleaving C₁
D₂: disp_bicat_of_opcleaving C₂
FF₁: D₁ -->[ F₁] D₂
FF₂: D₁ -->[ F₂] D₂
αα: disp_2cells α FF₁ FF₂
Hαα: ∏ (x : C₁ : univalent_category)
(xx : (pr1 D₁ : disp_univalent_category C₁) x),
is_opcartesian ((pr11 αα) x xx)
G: bicat_of_univ_cats
⟦ total_univalent_category (pr1 D₁),
total_univalent_category (pr1 D₂) ⟧
tot_FF₁:= total_functor (pr1 FF₁): bicat_of_univ_cats
⟦ total_univalent_category (pr1 D₁),
total_univalent_category (pr1 D₂) ⟧
tot_FF₂:= total_functor (pr1 FF₂): bicat_of_univ_cats
⟦ total_univalent_category (pr1 D₁),
total_univalent_category (pr1 D₂) ⟧
tot_αα:= total_nat_trans (pr1 αα): tot_FF₁ ==> tot_FF₂
γ: tot_FF₁ ==> G
δp: tot_FF₂ · pr1_category (pr1 D₂) ==>
G · pr1_category (pr1 D₂)
q: post_whisker γ (pr1_category (pr11 D₂)) =
nat_trans_comp
  (functor_composite_data
     (total_functor (pr1 FF₁))
     (pr1_category (pr1 D₂)))
  (functor_composite_data
     (total_functor (pr1 FF₂))
     (pr1_category (pr1 D₂)))
  (G · pr1_category (pr1 D₂))
  (post_whisker (total_nat_trans (pr1 αα))
     (pr1_category (pr1 D₂))) δp
x: total_univalent_category (pr1 D₁)
isaset (C₂ ⟦ F₁ (pr1 x), pr1 (G x) ⟧)

      apply homset_property.
  Qed.

     (total_functor (pr1 FF₁))
     (pr1_category (pr1 D₂)))
  (functor_composite_data
     (total_functor (pr1 FF₂))
     (pr1_category (pr1 D₂)))
  (G · pr1_category (pr1 D₂))
  (post_whisker (total_nat_trans (pr1 αα))
     (pr1_category (pr1 D₂))) δp

δ ▹ pr1_category (pr1 D₂) = δp × tot_αα • δ = γ

  (! base_paths ((tot_αα • pr1 φ₂) x) (γ x)
       (nat_trans_eq_pointwise (pr22 φ₂) x))
  (pr2 (γ x)) =

     (nat_trans_eq_pointwise (pr12 φ₁) x @
      ! nat_trans_eq_pointwise (pr12 φ₂) x))

     (! base_paths ((tot_αα • pr1 φ₁) x) (γ x)
          (nat_trans_eq_pointwise (pr22 φ₁) x))
     (pr2 (γ x)))

p:= opcleaving_of_opcleaving_opcartesian_2cell_is_pointwise_opcartesian
  αα Hαα: ∏ (x : C₁ : univalent_category)
(xx : (pr1 D₁ : disp_univalent_category C₁) x),
is_opcartesian ((pr11 αα) x xx)
G: bicat_of_univ_cats
⟦ total_univalent_category (pr1 D₁),
total_univalent_category (pr1 D₂) ⟧
γ: total_functor (pr1 FF₁) ==> G
δp: total_functor (pr1 FF₂) · pr1_category (pr1 D₂) ==>
G · pr1_category (pr1 D₂)
q: γ ▹ pr1_category (pr1 D₂) =
(total_nat_trans (pr1 αα) ▹ pr1_category (pr1 D₂))
• δp
(λ _ : local_opcartesian_opcleaving_lift α αα p G γ δp
         q ▹ pr1_category (pr1 D₂) = δp,
 total_nat_trans (pr1 αα)
 • local_opcartesian_opcleaving_lift α αα p G γ δp q =
 γ)
  (local_opcartesian_opcleaving_lift_over α αα p G γ
     δp q)
 exact (local_opcartesian_opcleaving_lift_comm α αα p G γ δp q).
Defined.
